  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a3bdea08-ab67-4c4e-b75c-b376f2e5c588'

  <span id="freeText13713209348105599865" style="display:none"><em>Don’t love your enemy. Declare war on him.</em><br /><br />Seventeen-year-old Isis Blake hasn’t fallen in love in three years, nine weeks, and five days, and after what happened last time, she intends to keep it that way. Since then she’s lost eighty-five pounds, gotten four streaks of purple in her hair, and moved to Buttcrack-of-Nowhere, Ohio, to help her mom escape a bad relationship.<br /><br />All the girls in her new school want one thing—Jack Hunter, the Ice Prince of East Summit High. Hot as an Armani ad, smart enough to get into Yale, and colder than the Arctic, Jack Hunter's never gone out with anyone. Sure, people have seen him downtown with beautiful women, but he's never given high school girls the time of day. Until Isis punches him in the face.<br /><br />Jack’s met his match. Suddenly everything is a game.<br /><br /><strong>The goal:</strong> Make the other beg for mercy.<br /><strong>The game board:</strong> East Summit High.<br /><strong>The reward:</strong> Something neither of them expected.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9829327990501849913"><b>MY EXACT REACTION TOWARDS THE END!!! YEP THIS WAS BASICALLY ME!!!</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386944797ra/7489024.gif' width='370' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I MEAN THAT ENDING!!!! ESPECIALLY THAT CLIFFHANGER LEFT ME...... JUST......</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361913.gif' width='370' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I mean, seriously, just.....<b>ugh!!!!!!!!!</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418564ra/828862.gif' width='370' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay okay let us rewind!! I stumbled upon this book while looking for new books to read. When I read the title, I was a little intrigued. Aside from the title being near to The Maine's (my favorite band) acoustic single <i>Lovely Sad</i>, the fact that the words lovely and vicious were put together really piqued my interest. </span>
  <span id="freeText9829327990501849913" style="display:none"><b>MY EXACT REACTION TOWARDS THE END!!! YEP THIS WAS BASICALLY ME!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386944797ra/7489024.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I MEAN THAT ENDING!!!! ESPECIALLY THAT CLIFFHANGER LEFT ME...... JUST......</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361913.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mean, seriously, just.....<b>ugh!!!!!!!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418564ra/828862.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay okay let us rewind!! I stumbled upon this book while looking for new books to read. When I read the title, I was a little intrigued. Aside from the title being near to The Maine's (my favorite band) acoustic single <i>Lovely Sad</i>, the fact that the words lovely and vicious were put together really piqued my interest. So then and there, I read the blurb and in no time, I started reading it. <br><br><b>AND READING IT WAS A GREAT DECISION!!!</b> Let's just say I was having a bad reading streak, and I just wanted to read something that I can't stop reading.....and this came along, soooo... YIPPEEEE!!!!<br><br>First of, Isis....<b>YOU CRACK ME UP EVERY SINGLE TIME!!!!!!!!!</b> All her schenanigans and the way she talks and the way she acts and practically everything she does makes me laugh my lungs out!!! Especially, the crazy antics she does because of her "war" with hottie Jack Hunter!!! I basically laughed my way throughout this book. <br><br>I was like this every single time:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386948266ra/7489885.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386948267ra/7489886.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>YUP JUST PLAIN HYSTERICAL!!! I MEAN WHO CAN BLAME ME?!?! IT WAS THAT FUNNY HAHAHAHAHAHAHHAHA!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384010333ra/6743615.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But even though Isis was tough and confident on the outside, she was really vulnerable and insecure on the inside. She used to be a lot bigger and she even considers herself <i>ugly</i>. And the main reason for this: <i>Nameless</i>. Ever since he hurt her, she hasn't fallen in love for three years, nine weeks, and five days. She promises to herself that she'll never fall in love again after the incident with <i>Nameless</i>. That is why when she moves with her mother to Ohio, she changes herself to someone more confident and more feisty, especially after she lost weight and dyed purple streaks to her hair.<br><br><b>This is where Mr. Ice Prince of East Summit High enters and saves the day!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390547378ra/8242000.gif" width="260" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack Hunter is popular and every girl's dream and every boy's envy.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403599ra/785146.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because he doesn't interact much, he was dubbed as the Ice Prince. <b>BUT ALAS HE MET HIS MATCH!!!</b> No other than little Ms. Hellion better known as Isis. Nobody can get on Jack's nerves better than Isis and vice versa. They start a very competitive war and begin to hate on each other BIGTIME! But we all know what happens when you hate someone a little too much.....<br><i>
  <blockquote>"I reach out for his hand, my own trembling. His fingers look so long and slender, and gentle. They feel smooth, and warm. I take hold of a few of them, like they’re a lifeline. A raft in the sea. A rope in a deep hole."</blockquote>
</i> <br><b>YUPPPP I WAS SWOONING FOR THE MOST PART, TOO!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/632033.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398860ra/771207.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380747943ra/3118900.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I MEAN THE ICE PRINCE WAS DELICIOUSLY HOT!!!!</b> And rude, arrogant and impossible!!.... But also very sweet and caring. <i>*cue swooning*</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/488595.gif" width="370" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>YEP JACK HUNTER WAS SWOON-MATERIAL!!!</b> Especially when he told Isis she was beautiful.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/672155.gif" width="340" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Isis was like:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386948267ra/7489887.gif" width="340" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, if you ask me if I'll ever order me some piece of that luscious Ice Prince.....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417914ra/827085.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Plus the other characters: Wren, Kayla, Avery, that crazy knife-dude, Evans, those weirdo teachers, their mothers, and even Sophia...They really added a different but nice touch to the story. THUMBS UP!!!<br><br>And me being a sucker for love-hate relationships, it was not difficult to enjoy and eventually love this book. Definitely made me smile, swoon, laugh, and everything in between <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386948267ra/7489888.gif" width="340" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>BUT THEN THAT ENDING</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386948267ra/7489889.gif" width="340" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I mean, 5 LOVELY AND VICIOUS STARSSSS!!! But then, yknow until the second book....</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400061ra/774834.gif" width="350" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[2016 May 28: Reread this again!!! Still great as ever!]</span>
  <a data-text-id="9829327990501849913" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1637333240" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16220020777388539091">Update 10-14-2017<br/><br/><br/><b>UNSAFE READ ALERT! OTHER WOMAN DRAMA </b><br/><b>UNSAFE READ ALERT! OTHER WOMAN DRAMA </b><br/><br/><br/>Dropping two stars and maybe dropping the series for good.<br/><br/>Spoiler for this book and the sequels <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Jack, the hero, works as a escort and at first I was okay with that because, he says that sex is rarely part of his job, he says that women usually hire him for non-sex stuff, like for making exes jealous or him going with them to proms and events. Stupid me! I believed him! I'm trying to read bo</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16220020777388539091" style="display:none">Update 10-14-2017<br><br><br><b>UNSAFE READ ALERT! OTHER WOMAN DRAMA </b><br><b>UNSAFE READ ALERT! OTHER WOMAN DRAMA </b><br><br><br>Dropping two stars and maybe dropping the series for good.<br><br>Spoiler for this book and the sequels <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Jack, the hero, works as a escort and at first I was okay with that because, he says that sex is rarely part of his job, he says that women usually hire him for non-sex stuff, like for making exes jealous or him going with them to proms and events. Stupid me! I believed him! I'm trying to read book 2 and after Jack and Isis kiss he not only keeps his job but his relationship with an ex-flame is stronger than I thought. If you don't like love triangles F/M/F avoid this series. That's a shame because Isis is one of my favorite heroines, she has serious self-esteem issues and she hides behind her humorous facade to try to survive. A heroine like her deserved better! Please don't tell me that's not cheating because he's not officialy dating Isis! It's 100% disloyal and stupid! I hate it.<br><br>Also he kind of dates platonically (at Isis insistance) one of heroine's best friends. It's a very platonic relationship that seems to be only to make Isis happy, but now that I know he's so close to Sophia I see his dating Kayla as weak, disloyal and traitorous.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>I'm taking back everything nice I said about Jack Hunter. I'm so glad I didn't pay for book two! <br><br><br>Original review. I feel tempted to erase it, but my friends liked it already so I won't eraset I'll just hide under spoilers.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[LUCAS TILL AS JACK HUNTER!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474408334i/20595343._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4 I-couldn't-stop-reading-I-couldn't-stop laughing stars </b><br>Thank you so much The dreamer for the book recommendation. I loved it.<br>I thought that Cassandra Clare, J.K Rowling, and Jennifer L. Armentrout were the authors to go when you want to read cute bantering and female characters with the wittiest comebacks. I was wrong. Not even Isabelle Lightwood can contest Isis Blake's sass. The first 50% of the book was text-book of how to write a heroine with the smartest comebacks and the sassiest dialogue. Even her internal monologues were so entertaining. And she spoke some of her internal monologue aloud! Even better: she never became embarrassed about it! She's crazy like that. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474417559ra/20596355.gif" width="800" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Practically every page of the first half of the book is full of funny dialogue. I don't recommend reading this in public. It's very difficult to keep a straight face while reading this book.<br><br>That's not to say that I didn't find problems with this book. I'll address those later, but the fact that the protagonist Isis Blake is a Gem difficult to find in contemporary "romance" (notice the quotations in romance, I'll address that later) makes me want to give not 5 but 6 stars.<br><br>Isis Blake is a force of nature. One of the most complex heroines I've read in recent years. She's completly and unapologetically crazy, she can be as immature and childish as a 5-year-old one minute, and a very loyal friend the next. She can plant weed on a locker to get revenge of her enemies and then go home to cook dinner and take care of her depressed mother. She could be the girl you'd like to be your friend or the crazy freak you'd want to keep at an arm's length because she's just so unpredictable and so unapologetic. I personally wanted to hug her and offer her comfort.<br>From the moment I read the first pages and the way Isis feels about love I knew that she had been hurt, both physically and emotionally and that all that humor, all those contradictory attitudes (one minute she calls herself ugly and feels insecure, another minute someone tries to bully her and she'll rise to the occasion by jokingly calling herself "hot") seemed to be rooted in her need to fight against the people who hurt her, against her internal demons, against her tragic past. I really got to understand her character and to feel as though she could be any girl I know. She's like a young Lorelai Gilmore (watch the Gilmore girls if you haven't) Lisbet Salender (watch the girl with the dragon tatoo Fincher's version) Buffy the Vampire slayer, and Jenna Hamilton from Awkward. Except Isis is wittier, sassier and way much more broken inside than all the other women I mentioned.<br><br>Maybe it's not so much that she's so strong as much of the fact that she's constant and true to herself and never acts OCC. To be honest I've read contemporary heroines that are sassy and strong, too. The problem is that at some point they act stupidly or more like the authors make them act stupidly. Isis can be silly at times, but never stupid. That wasn't a problem with this book, although there were other problems, but none of them were major for me. The hero compensated for that and now I don't even know if I should enter into detail into those problems as they are very personal. I feel most readers wont' have any problems reading this book unless they hate dark topics. Even if you don't relate or like the heroine at the very least I'm sure you'll finish the book quickly and be thoroughly entertained and laughing and enjoying the crazy situations. This is a good mix of comedy and dark topics.<br><br>I love Jack Hunter. He reminds me so much of another favorite of mine Aleksey from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21799202-the-v-girl" rel="nofollow noopener">The V Girl</a> UPDATE, I TAKE THAT BACK! JACK ISN'T LOYAL and he has eyes for other women !!!hate him!! I'm recommending this book to my group of friends who love Aleksey as much as I do. The leonine silent attitude. The fact that Jack's not a manwhore. He's a silent, broody jackass that can also be very caring. He challenges the heroine and protects her at the same time and their first encounter is in a situation in which both are in opposite sides of the war. He can be hurtful one minute and then dress as Jack Sparrow the next because he knows that SHE is crazy for (and as crazy as) Jack Sparrow. I love that so much. My only problem with him is that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ unlike Aleksey who never loved anyone else, Jack seems too attached to a girl in his past. It's clear that he loves her in a way that isn't clear to me, does he love OW as a sister? or does he have other feelings? Love triangles aren't my thing. If he's really into that girl (I'm crossing finger the sequel won't be about that) I think he might enter the category of disloyal heroes, because he kind of dates one of Isis's friends (not exactly date, more like letting the girl kiss him so the friend would be happy and Isis would lower her guard and smile more) and I don't know if he's being disloyal or not to this other girl. And if he really loved her at one point that will ruin the book for me. I want him to love only Isis. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>WARNINGS with potential spoilers: This book follows the tendency of late to include strong language, dark situations (prostitution, PSTD, rape attempt, date rape attempt, suicide, bullying, drugs) in a YA read. There's no nudity or sexual situations (a descriptive make out with clothes on happens) , but just beware that lately YA romance is becoming more and more edgy. Also at the end of the book some situations will require your suspension of disbelief. <br><br>I'm recommending this book to fans of the enemies to lovers trope and fans of cute banter and slow burners. Perhaps also the fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16113791" rel="nofollow noopener"> The coincidence of Kayden and Callie</a> will enjoy this book (because there's pain behind the MC's attitudes) and the fans of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28678119" rel="nofollow noopener"> Paper princess</a> will enjoy the love-hate relationship and the reality-show-soap-opera situations full of drama.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Taking back everything I said about the romance in my original review, the 3 stars are all for Isis! That girl deserved more! After all the pain she went through, it's so unfair.<br><br>I'm upset! This is the last time I read unfinished contempoary series. I swear! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cheating  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> in the sequels is the worst!<br><br>Read if you want to laugh, but don't expect a loyal hero.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16220020777388539091" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/765591876?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kimsandara" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kimsandara" href="/user/show/11129715-kimsandara">Kimsandara</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11129715-kimsandara?shelf=blah-read">blah-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11129715-kimsandara?shelf=hated-it">hated-it</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11129715-kimsandara?shelf=epic-waste-of-time">epic-waste-of-time</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer765591876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17653482983750695967">I'll give it to you in a few words:<br/><br/><u>Predictable</u><br/>Girl had a massive trauma in her past<br/>Girl changed and wanted to start over<br/>Girl meets this incredibly sexy dude<br/>(Dude is cold and detached. Here Dude is nicknamed "The Ice Prince")<br/>Girl thinks she hates dude<br/>Girl falls in love with dude<br/><br/><u>Over the top</u><br/>Dude has massive traumatic past too (that's why he is cold)<br/>Dude linked to a mysterious girl <br/>(Girl is curious about/jealous of mysterious girl)<br/>Mysterious girl's past is traumatic/disturbing<br/>+ She is ill like deat</span>
  <span id="freeText17653482983750695967" style="display:none">I'll give it to you in a few words:<br /><br /><u>Predictable</u><br />Girl had a massive trauma in her past<br />Girl changed and wanted to start over<br />Girl meets this incredibly sexy dude<br />(Dude is cold and detached. Here Dude is nicknamed "The Ice Prince")<br />Girl thinks she hates dude<br />Girl falls in love with dude<br /><br /><u>Over the top</u><br />Dude has massive traumatic past too (that's why he is cold)<br />Dude linked to a mysterious girl <br />(Girl is curious about/jealous of mysterious girl)<br />Mysterious girl's past is traumatic/disturbing<br />+ She is ill like death-inducing ill...<br />Girl's mama also has a traumatic past (...)<br />Dude is pimping himself out (while his family is supposedly rich)to help someone out. Seems a good reason but stupid in the end (ask Mummy for money?)<br /><br /><u>Superficial</u><br />Girl is frenenemy with pretty-ass Queen bee<br />Love triangle with "bestfriend"(do I need to develop?)<br />Immature humour/reaction (Girl throws poop at Boy's car; Girl/Boy fall into a fountain full of piss -_-)<br /><br /><u>Impossible</u><br />High School director plasters pictures of girl when she was fat on the walls for a reason(HAHAHAHA) <br />Girl storms into class to yell at Boy. Teacher does nothing but oogle girl in skimpy attire.<br />Girl plants drugs into boy's locker to ruin his reputation(Impossibly idiotic) <br /><br />And the list goes on and on. This crap may have been funny when I was seven, but I have grown older!<br />The writing was amateurish and plain stupid at times. Err, never again!<br /><br />---------------------------- Edited-----------------------------------<br />I do realise that I sound very harsh in this review and honestly I generally try not to be mean toward the writers and the readers that actually liked a book that I dislike. Here, 95% of the readers did like Lovely Vicious. <br /><br />The main reason why I think this book shouldn't have been printed in the first place is that there is no semblance of realism. It reads like a badly written fanfiction. I wager the writer had a great time writing it but the plot (what plot?) goes nowhere. It is a string of awkward situations and maudlin dialogues.<br /><br /> I don't have anything against suspending my disbelief for a while but Sara Wolf went too far. <br />So yes, Lovely Vicious was a huge disappointement for me. </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/877497808?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18856964-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=its-funny-ahahaha">its-funny-ahahaha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=give-this-author-a-bells">give-this-author-a-bells</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=its-the-drama-in-the-llama">its-the-drama-in-the-llama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=it-hurts-in-my-heart">it-hurts-in-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=mental-illness">mental-illness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=words-cannot-explain">words-cannot-explain</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer877497808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10442386981356097808"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410607602i/11130293.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Whenever I finish reading an amazing book, I clam up! I have no idea how to express my feelings. So yeah, I loved this book so so so much!<br/><br/>As depressing as the quote above is, I wasn't really depressed by this book. Maybe sad and at times a little tearful, but this book was a medley of teen angst covered in some pretty wicked humour. First and foremost I should probably stress that I do love teen angst, all kinds of it! I love going through the awkwardness, unnecessary self loathing and torturous</span>
  <span id="freeText10442386981356097808" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410607602i/11130293.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Whenever I finish reading an amazing book, I clam up! I have no idea how to express my feelings. So yeah, I loved this book so so so much!<br><br>As depressing as the quote above is, I wasn't really depressed by this book. Maybe sad and at times a little tearful, but this book was a medley of teen angst covered in some pretty wicked humour. First and foremost I should probably stress that I do love teen angst, all kinds of it! I love going through the awkwardness, unnecessary self loathing and torturous romance... in books.<br><br>I loved, Isis! She has some serious issues but don't for one minute think that she's a doormat because of it. She was loud, obnoxious, opinionated, smart, witty and incredibly loyal to her friend Kayla. Even though I couldn't stand Kayla. Isis is a transfer student, so she's the new girl and reformed fat girl. At her old school she was known as the fat girl, a boy she calls Nameless broke her heart and she can't stand to hear his name said. She lives with her mother who was recently physically assaulted by her ex-boyfriend. Her mother suffers from PTSD, and Isis has become the parent and her mother the child (my personal observation). So she they've move and she's started a new school and goes to her first party. Which is where it all begins...with a kiss.<br><br><b>
  <i>I like to think being genuinely nice is one of my strengths though, you know, minus punching guys who deserve it. So I'll be nice. I'll keep myself from everyone else. No one wants ugly. Even if they did, it wouldn't be good for them. I'm loud and angry and sarcastic. No one wants that. Nameless taught me that too. He taught me to spare everyone from myself. That's true kindness.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410607602i/11130294.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enter Jack AKA The Ice Prince. Breaker of many hearts and doesn't give a shit about it either. Actually he probably isn't even aware of it, Isis zeroes in on him, while her friend Kayla continues her 6 year crush fest on him. Jack hurts Kayla's feelings, Isis is put out on behalf of her friend and vows to make him apologise, and so a war begins. Who will out smart the other?<br><br><b>
  <u>My Thoughts</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408759050ra/10893481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isis, is the epitome of an outcast. She doesn't fit in anywhere, but then again she doesn't feel like she has to. There's some bullying and threats but she never takes it lying down. Isis fought all the way, I wanted to smack her at times because her loyalty to Kayla was infuriating. Kayla may have been sweet but she was also selfish, and even blatantly abused Isis' friendship.<br><br>This book does not deal with light subject matter, but it does address it with humour which I did appreciate. Nothing was trivialised but it's really difficult reading about a depressed and whiney heroine. Isis, was a breathe of fresh air.<br><br>So if you're looking for a YA book, with some drama, angst, romance and hilarious and smart banter this is your book! </span>
  <a data-text-id="10442386981356097808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1532897177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14795497788580738288"><br/><pre>
  <b>**5 captivating stars!!**</b>
</pre><br/><br/>I do not understand why I loved this book this much. <br/>I.Could.Not.Stop.Reading it. <br/>I was hooked by Isis's <s>crazy</s> voice, <br/>funny banters, <br/>and <s>fake</s> personality. <br/><br/><pre><b>➀</b> This book deals with dark issues:<br/>✦ Weight loss.<br/>✦ Low Self Esteem.<br/>✦ A dark mysterious past. <br/>✦ Friends.<br/>✦ Fitting in. <br/>✦ Mental health issues. <br/>✦ Bad Break ups. </pre><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. <br/>Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. <br/>You can’t always wait like that. <br/>You have to</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText14795497788580738288" style="display:none"><br><pre>
  <b>**5 captivating stars!!**</b>
</pre><br><br>I do not understand why I loved this book this much. <br>I.Could.Not.Stop.Reading it. <br>I was hooked by Isis's <s>crazy</s> voice, <br>funny banters, <br>and <s>fake</s> personality. <br><br><pre><b>➀</b> This book deals with dark issues:<br>✦ Weight loss.<br>✦ Low Self Esteem.<br>✦ A dark mysterious past. <br>✦ Friends.<br>✦ Fitting in. <br>✦ Mental health issues. <br>✦ Bad Break ups. </pre><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. <br>Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. <br>You can’t always wait like that. <br>You have to seek out change on your own.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>➁ </b>I might've enjoyed this book because it reminded me of anime. <br>And as you might know, or not know, I adore anime. <br>This book's characters were a lot like anime characters. <br><br>✦<i>The Nerdy anime character with <br>big glasses, <br>vast knowledge, <br>and also popularity at some point:<br><b>Wren!</b></i><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/26bce6e0056ac64ee1939a910f3ee8c11294437447_full_1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454366077i/17950902.jpg" alt=" photo 26bce6e0056ac64ee1939a910f3ee8c11294437447_full_1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>✦ The girl who has boys lusting for her.<br>She's the popular<br><i>nice</i> girl. <br><i>
  <b>Kayla</b>
</i> <br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/superthumb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454366077i/17950903.jpg" alt=" photo superthumb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>✦ The arrogant mean girl who controls everyone. <br>She's not liked, <br>but for some reason, <br>people follow her blindly. <br>She's good looking, <br>rich,<br>and very mean in a way <br><i>that can lock someone in jail</i>,<br>not bullying mean if you know what I mean. <br><b>
  <i>Avery</i>
</b> <br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/bow-brown-eyes-brown-hair-hair-bow-kimono-lips-long-hair-noizi-ito-solo-wafuku-zoom-layer-anime-girl-pretty-beautiful-art-wallpaper-orange-hair-autumn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454366077i/17950904._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo bow-brown-eyes-brown-hair-hair-bow-kimono-lips-long-hair-noizi-ito-solo-wafuku-zoom-layer-anime-girl-pretty-beautiful-art-wallpaper-orange-hair-autumn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>✦ The smart mysterious guy. <br>Girls love him for his looks. <br>Guys respect him for his intelligence. <br>Teachers love him for his grades. <br>He has a bad reputation, <br>but everyone still love him regardless of his <br><s> crazy</s> personality. <br>The guy isn't nice, <br>and doesn't sugar coat anything. <br>He's mean to girls, <br>and rude to everyone. <br>Yet, he's still very popular <br>&amp; well loved by everyone. <br>This character is very common in the anime world. <br><i>
  <b>Jack!</b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/Anime-anime-boy-beautiful-boy-Favim.com-647312_1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454366077i/17950905._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Anime-anime-boy-beautiful-boy-Favim.com-647312_1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>✦ The new girl. <br>A girl who's funny and loved. <br>She grab people's attention. <br>She's loud, <br>crazy, <br>and fun. <br>Yet, she's wise, <br>caring, <br>and thankful. <br>She has very serious issues, <br>and her funky personality is just there <br>to mask the <s>real</s> her. <br>She's running away from problems, <br>and in reality, <br>she's very <s>scared</s>. <br>No matter how much she goes through, <br>she's still strong &amp; ready to fight.<br><i>
  <b>Isis.</b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/tumblr_ni8ydbB1UY1u55xnmo1_400.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454366077ra/17950906.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ni8ydbB1UY1u55xnmo1_400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I would love to slap you right now, <br>but I’m currently wielding a nine pound ball and I’m afraid that would be called murder.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>➂</b> I might've been in love with this novel because <br>Jack &amp; Isis's love story wasn't instant. <br>I just despite <i>instant-love</i> stories. <br>I see it as a <b>curse</b> done by the author. <br>Ok I might be exaggerating a bit, <br>but I honestly don't like instant love in my books <br>because it's unrealistic &amp; makes me want to roll my eyes. <br>Repeatedly. <br>Jack &amp; Isis's relationship grew slowly from <i>nothing, <br>to hate, <br>to war, <br>to sympathy, <br>caring, <br>and then finally attraction</i>. <br>They slowly started liking each other. <br>It wasn't instant, <br>and I must admit, <br>it was kind of very <s>slow</s> nice. <br><br><b><blockquote>“How did you find me? If you hacked into the Club’s computer to look up my appointments-"<br>“Whoa, I think you overestimate me, shitlord. Last time I checked all I did was be in the wrong place at the right time. I saw you and had to - ”<br>“Stalk me.”<br>“ - delicately approach you. In a sideways manner. From behind. Without being seen at all. For ten minutes.”</blockquote> </b><br><br><b>➃</b> I don't know why I did this, <br>but I was on the edge of my seat the whole time. <br>Actually, <br>I was supposed to read a bit before my bed time, <br>but when I held it and started reading, <br>I dropped it <b>only after</b> I was done with it. <br>I read the whole book in one sitting. <br>I didn't even update my GR 'currently reading' list. <br>I was so consumed, <br>and struck by this book from the moment I held it. <br>In the end, I slept <i>very</i> late, <br>but I don't regret what I did even though I had to wake up early the next morning. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“And then he came, <br>and pulled her petals off one by one, <br>forcing her to surround herself with thorns to survive. <br>But he missed one petal.<br> And she guards it with a tiger's ferocity.” <br>
</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>➄</b> I might've also loved this book because of the<br>Japanese words thrown here and there. <br>As I said, <br>I'm a big Anime fan, <br>and in return, <br>I learned a little Japanese on my free time. <br>So seeing Japanese words thrown here and there, <br>and actually understanding what it meant <br>without reading the meaning just made me feel <i>awesome.</i> <br>I know. <br>That's irrelevant, <br>but I want to share my enthusiasm with the world. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Because I’m strong. <br>Because I’m Isis Blake, <br>and she might not be pretty, <br>or sweet, <br>or well-mannered, <br>but she’s very, very strong.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>➅</b> The plot was so<i> unpredictable</i>. <br>I enjoyed reading every part of it. <br>There were many plot twists I didn't see coming, <br>which only made me enjoy the book more. <br>I liked how Jack and Isis were both very observant and smart. <br>I love how the writer surprised us with every secret revealed. <br>The writing was mostly in Isis's POV, <br>and it was hilarious. <br>Jack's POV was a bit <s>darker</s>, <br>and more obvious than Isis. <br>Regardless, the book was full of humor despite the dark themes. <br><br><b>“Hello, spawn!” I coo at Kayla’s baby brother as he waddles into her room. He burps at me.<br>“It looks like you guys speak the same language,” Kayla quips.<br>“Where was that sass when Jack was making you cry at Avery’s party?”<br>“Uh, hello? He’s my crush? I’m not going to sass him.”<br>“Flash ‘em the sass before you flash ‘em the ass.”<br>“What kind of saying is that?” She laughs.<br>“Grandma-saying. She’s the head of the motorcycle gang at her nursing home.” </b><br><br><b>➆</b> The <i>freaking <b>ending</b></i>. <br>I was like WTF? <br>Also the part where <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Jack goes crazy &amp; beat Leo so hard and is actually very excited about it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br>I was terrified of that scene honestly. <br>Now I'm not sure how to feel. <br><br>Now that I have gushed, <br>and pointed out how great this book is, <br>I can go read the second book happily because I'm anticipating it so badly. <br><br>Also, I <b>recommend</b> this read to everyone because <br>it's funny, <br>cute, <br><s>dark</s>, <br>and mysterious all at the same time. <br>The characters are likable. <br>Even the queen bee isn't <i>that</i> bad. <br>The plot was refreshing and unpredictable. <br>The tone was very funny at times, <br>and very dark at times. <br>This book <b>has it all.</b> So yes, <br><br>I <b>recommend it to <i>everyone.</i></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="chan ☆" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48727754-chan"><img alt="chan ☆" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596680961p2/48727754.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2687873233?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="chan ☆" class="user" itemprop="url" name="chan ☆" href="/user/show/48727754-chan">chan ☆</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=2019">2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=ya-contemporary">ya-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=problematic">problematic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=the-worst">the-worst</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2687873233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5871076539434911636"><b>if after by anna todd had a funny love child</b><br/><br/>good god this was horrific, and i'm honestly kicking myself for not taking any notes. it seemed like on every page there was something to laugh at and criticize. you might notice there are 2 stars and not 1 up there. but that's because this book was actually funny. let me break it all down for you:<br/><br/><b>what was good(ish)</b><br/><br/>this was fucking funny. and i don't mean that in a "i'm laughing at you" sort of way. i was genuinely entertained for the first like 40% of</span>
  <span id="freeText5871076539434911636" style="display:none"><b>if after by anna todd had a funny love child</b><br /><br />good god this was horrific, and i'm honestly kicking myself for not taking any notes. it seemed like on every page there was something to laugh at and criticize. you might notice there are 2 stars and not 1 up there. but that's because this book was actually funny. let me break it all down for you:<br /><br /><b>what was good(ish)</b><br /><br />this was fucking funny. and i don't mean that in a "i'm laughing at you" sort of way. i was genuinely entertained for the first like 40% of the book. both the internal and external dialogue in this book were pretty damn good. constant funny metaphors, zingers, etc. i was pleased. but that's about it. because it started annoying me after the 40% mark, along with a dozen other things<br /><br /><b>what sucked ass</b><br /><br />where to fucking start. first of all: the entire premise of this book is silly af. this girl decides to wage a war against a guy at her new school because she doesn't like that this guy is "rude." and by rude she means that he doesn't pay attention to the girls that are interested in him. but from everything that we know of jack he isn't a dickhead. he just wants to be left the fuck alone.<br /><br />but of course isis decides that she wants to be an asshole to this dude because she has been burned one too many times by guys. she harasses the fuck out of him and is surprised when he retaliates. honestly i felt kind of sorry for this guy, he has his own stuff going on and she had to poke the sleeping bear.<br /><br /><b>but beyond the absolutely idiotic plot we've got so many things that never would have happened in real life. let's list them shall we</b><br /><br />- principal posting your "fat" pics from before you got skinny, all over the school<br />- principal applying to colleges on your behalf<br />- mean girl giving her friend a date rape drug so a guy might take advantage of her<br />- mean girl trying to appropriate school funds to go on a trip to france to get back an estranged friend<br />- a 17 year old male escorting to pay a friend's medical bills<br />- a straight-out-of-soap-operas amnesia cliffhanger<br /><br />those are just some that i can think of off the top of my head. every twist and turn is laughably stupid and i just kept hitting my head saying <b>why</b> every time something new happened.<br /><br />blessedly, i have a friend who is going to continue this series and keep me informed on all of the dumb things that happen. but thankfully i won't be reading.<br /><br /><b>(also why did every one of my goodreads friends rate this 4+ stars i'm honestly speechless</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1671036200?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE</span></div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1671036200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16612892585358864814"><b> 6 incredible stars!! </b><br/><br/>This story is remarkable and unforgettable! It caught my attention and just sucked me in without a care in the world! This story is about a girl named Isis, who moves from Florida to Ohio to start over little did she know that she would start a war with Jack the Ice Prince + coping with the past+ taking care of her mother. Isis and Jack are both mastermind, conniving people but that only makes the events and banter that happen between them so much more hilarious and heart g</span>
  <span id="freeText16612892585358864814" style="display:none"><b> 6 incredible stars!! </b><br><br>This story is remarkable and unforgettable! It caught my attention and just sucked me in without a care in the world! This story is about a girl named Isis, who moves from Florida to Ohio to start over little did she know that she would start a war with Jack the Ice Prince + coping with the past+ taking care of her mother. Isis and Jack are both mastermind, conniving people but that only makes the events and banter that happen between them so much more hilarious and heart grabbing. I fell in love with them individually and together. This story was refreshing and new for me and Sarah Wolf, you did a fantastic job at making me so happy and then <b> CRUSHING IT! WHAT KIND OF ENDING WAS THAT!?!! YOU CAN’T JUST HAVE A CLIFFHANGER LIKE THAT AND EXPECT ME TO BE SANE AFTER IT!? </b><br><br>Chapter sixteen:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466282556ra/19462644.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Chapter seventeen:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447187491ra/16967185.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Cliffhanger:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1461075426ra/18820271.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> *tries to calm myself down* </i> Back to what I was saying this is a must read. I might be late on reading this trilogy, but that just means there are a lot of others that are late as well so join the bandwagon, my friends, you won’t regret it… well you’ll regret it once you get to the cliffhanger BUT it will all be wort-.. you know what just read the damn book and be as mesmerized as I am!<br><br><b> This book includes:<br>Funny banter<br>Weight loss <br>Friendship<br>Cliffhanger (*rolls eyes*)<br>Insecurities <br>Total Swoonage<br>Romance<br>Drama<br>Dark secrets<br>Mystery<br>Pain<br>Tears (cause my sappy ass cried)<br>Oh and Isis casually thinking out loud </b><br><br>Five of the Characters (More characters added an extremely nice touch to the book):<br><br><b> Isis </b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466284213i/19462830.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Isis is my <b> FAVORITE </b> heroine. She’s a girl I know I’d be best friends with in real life. You just have to like her right away even though she deals with a lot of issues and is running away from her past she’s stronger than she knows. She’s sarcastic, crazy, babbles a lot, caring, <b> INSANELY </b> hilarious and has an attention-grabbing personality. You never know what she’s going to say or do next, and that’s why I admire her. Ten pages in and you’ll fall in love with Isis. Why? She punches the Ice Prince; I mean Jack for being disrespectful to Kayla... a girl that wasn’t even her friend (yet). Isis doesn’t do disrespect, and she’ll make sure you know it, or her first will connect with your face in a matter of seconds, don’t believe me? Ask, Jack. He’ll tell you about it ;)<br><br><pre> <i> Say it. Say one more thing, pretty boy. I dare you to. </i> </pre><br><b> “You’re pathetic,” he says.<br>That’s the <i> first </i> time I punch Jack Hunter’s face.<br>And as my knuckles connect with his stupid high cheekbones and he staggers back with a furious blizzard brewing in his icy eyes. I somehow get the feeling It won’t be the last time.<br>“Apologize to Kayla,” I demand, and the entire house goes quiet. </b><br>(….)<br><b> “Judging by your expression” – I cross my arms and glower – “getting punched for being an ass Is something new.” </b> <br><br><b> Jack– Ice Prince </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466284564i/19462907.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The guy every girl wants to change and be with and every guy hates but wishes they were. Jack doesn’t talk much to anyone at his school; he keeps to himself which leads him to be mysterious <i>(I love him) </i>. No one’s ever crossed him until he meets Isis, his match made in heaven. They’re completely different but the same <i> (why do I love him so much?)</i>. Jack is cold, arrogant, beyond blunt, challenging and <b> RUDE </b> <i> (I just want him in my life) </i> But beneath that icy heart he’s actually a sweetheart and is caring but only to the ones he cares about <i> (Jack, hit me up) </i>. The rivalry between Jack and Isis hectic but they do have their pleasant moments. Let’s just say its all fair in love &amp; war ;)<br><br><b> “I’d tap the shit outta that ho.” A redheaded boy smacks the air in front of his crotch lasciviously. I don’t have time to stop myself –he’s pinned against the water fountain in less than two seconds.<br>“Repeat that,” I growl<br>“W-What?” the redhead stutters “C’mon man, let go!” <br>“Repeat what you just said,” I insist </b><br>(….)<br><b> I redirect my glare to the redhead. “If I hear you spewing your perverted bullshit about that girl again, well. Ask the football team why they avoid me, would you? It might enlighten you.” </b><br><br><i> Side note: When Jack is turned on (Halloween party)? WOAH BABY!! </i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418949292ra/12953134.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Kayla </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466284564i/19462908.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kayla is the girl that is popular, and you’d expect her to be a bitch because every guy wants her, but she’s sweet, kind, loyal and just quirky. But she doesn’t only want to be known as a beautiful face because she’s more than that.<br><br><b> “Just, you know. I’m nice. I can get things from people.”<br>“You’re pretty.”<br>“But I’m also nice! And I’m smart! Okay, maybe not in world history, but who even cares about stupid plagues anyway? We have vaccines now! I’m really good at home ec, and Gregory said I have a natural talent for calculus, okay? I’m a lot of things besides pretty, so don’t just say that like everyone else!” </b><br><br><b> Avery </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466284045i/19462819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Avery is Regina George, just a red head and worst.<br><br><b> “It’s incredible. I knew she was a bitch, but I had no idea she used to be a whale. Do you think she’s covered in stretch marks, or what? How much of her is flab?” Avery chuckles. </b><br><br><b> Wren </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466284564i/19462909.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Wren is the student council president, popular and is friends with everyone but is also intimidating<br><br><b> “I’m sorry.” Wren squints at me. “Do I know you? Oh, wait. I do know you The new girl. Isis Blake.”<br>“The one and only!” I smile<br>“July 1, 1998. Blood type 0 positive. You previously lived in Good Falls, Florida, with your aunt. You’re allergic to strawberries.”<br>I’m shocked, but I keep my smile. “How do you know so-“ <br>“I’ve read your school record. I volunteer in the office.” </b><br><br>I don’t know how I hadn’t read this book because It has just gone on my favorite list!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392995114ra/8644499.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more reviews, click below!<br><div> <a href="https://bookitwithdon.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465508902i/19367462._SX540_.png" alt="Book It With Don" width="275" height="140" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a> </div></b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1122817991?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=dnf">dnf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=annoying-heroines">annoying-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1122817991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1630309527258436570">DNF at 46%.<br/><br/>I'm so sorry, guys. And I'm so sorry, AJ, my friend, who recommended this to me. :((<br/><br/>It's just that... I really, really wanted to like this. But I just can't. I mean, I'm not the type of reader who does this DNF-ing thing, but I was forced because I can't tolerate the immaturity of this book. Yes, there was a ton of it and it was getting annoying every single second and it was already getting on my nerves to the point that I could no longer take it.<br/><br/>When I first met Isis at the beginnin</span>
  <span id="freeText1630309527258436570" style="display:none">DNF at 46%.<br /><br />I'm so sorry, guys. And I'm so sorry, AJ, my friend, who recommended this to me. :((<br /><br />It's just that... I really, really wanted to like this. But I just can't. I mean, I'm not the type of reader who does this DNF-ing thing, but I was forced because I can't tolerate the immaturity of this book. Yes, there was a ton of it and it was getting annoying every single second and it was already getting on my nerves to the point that I could no longer take it.<br /><br />When I first met Isis at the beginning chapter, I thought she was cool, funny, and brave-- a little sarcastic and snarky but tolerable, but as the story progressed, I realized she's difficult to like and get along with. She was no longer making any sense and she kept on whining about how bad she looks and how fat she was and how shaken she was when she was ditched by her ex and how insecure she is every time she encounters her chic school mates. Ugh! Isis is one of those characters that really pull the bitch out of me and make me roll my eyes every time.<br /><br />Jack, on the other hand, is-- I dunno. He's a likeable character but definitely not the one who could be labeled as a book boyfriend. He's always too passive and I think his character development is so poor I could not really connect with him.<br /><br />At some point I was trying to convince myself to continue it and read it up to the very final chapter to find out how it ends. I've read from reviews that it has a cliffhanger ending and I love cliffhangers because they're challenging but I no longer have the interest to continue.<br /><br />So yeah, this book unfortunately did not get me. Again, I'm sorry especially for the guys who loved this book. I really am. :(</span>
  <a data-text-id="1630309527258436570" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1053368060" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1053368060" />
    <a title="Lazaros" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros"><img alt="Lazaros" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578697302p2/22313662.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1053368060?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lazaros" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lazaros" href="/user/show/22313662-lazaros">Lazaros</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22313662-lazaros?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1053368060" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16579578876540998833"><i>
  <blockquote>«I reach out for his hand, my own trembling. His fingers look so long and slender, and gentle. They feel smooth, and warm. I take hold of a few of them, like they’re a lifeline. A raft in the sea.  A rope in a deep hole.<br/>“You smell good,” I say. “And you’re fun to pick on. And I like your mom. You’re smart. Kind of dumb, but also kind of smart. I had fun. With the war. And the kiss. And the date. And you called me beautiful and it was nice. So even if we never battle again, even if you hate me</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText16579578876540998833" style="display:none"><i>
  <blockquote>«I reach out for his hand, my own trembling. His fingers look so long and slender, and gentle. They feel smooth, and warm. I take hold of a few of them, like they’re a lifeline. A raft in the sea.  A rope in a deep hole.<br />“You smell good,” I say. “And you’re fun to pick on. And I like your mom. You’re smart. Kind of dumb, but also kind of smart. I had fun. With the war. And the kiss. And the date. And you called me beautiful and it was nice. So even if we never battle again, even if you hate me forever for saying I like you, thank you. Thank you a lot -»</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />If there's one thing I loved the most about this book, and trust me I loved lots of things about it, then it's the fact that Isis is one of the truest and kindest heroines I've ever had the pleasure of reading about. This entire book took me by surprise. It was so good, i enjoyed it thoroughly.<br /><br />Despite the bleak theme it targeted, which is that of abuse, I think the fact that the main character, Isis, is so funny and can make light of whatever situation she finds herself in. Her humor and self-sarcasm took the dark edge off the book and made me enjoy it that much more.<br /><br />Isis used to be the girl everyone made fun of. She was a target for ill comments about her weight. She used to be the girl on the sidelines, the girl who had lots of excess weight on and who got fat-shamed all the time. I'm sure many of you had girls like that at your school. Many of you might have been that girl or boy who everyone made fun of. Well, Isis got used in the worst possible way, she fell in love and the guy not only broke her heart but took advantage of her in the process and humiliated her.<br /><br />Her mom was beaten by her ex-boyfriend, so she and Iris have moved away and started a new life. Isis has lost all of her excess weight but she still doesn't trust anyone, especially boys. She still has self-confidence issues, she thinks she's ugly. She says that she's never going to love again. Isis is one of those people who try to make fun of everything, out of every situation, just so they can hide behind those jokes and jests. She doesn't want to face reality and she continually avoids dealing with her emotions.<br /><br />First day into the new school and she makes a friend but also an enemy. The friend is Kayla, and the enemy is Kayla's crush, named Jack. Jack is, shall I say the female version of Isis? Yes, he's colder, and distanced and has no friends at all but they're the same in the way that they both want to always be in control, of their life, of their emotions, and that's what ignites a war between them. She tries to hurt him and he retaliates. Uncovering secrets. Shaming one another. Spreading rumors about each other. Snarky comments and endlessly sassy retorts and funny comments. It's fun to witness that and I'll admit I laughed a lot while reading this.<br /><br />I felt for the characters, the main ones and the supporting ones. I connected with them and I got to experience their problems and empathize with them. The author did a very good job of conveying the characters' feelings and I'm still overwhelmed by the way it ended and it was all kinds of sad and heart-breaking and it makes me that much more eager to grab the next book and read it in one sitting till my eyes turn red from sleep deprivation. <br /><br />There's a lot of backstory and there are twists which honestly didn't see coming and this is really deep story and very unique, too. The characters have depth and this book was such a nice surprise and it was also sad but also thought-provocative and it's not one of those young-adult books that you read and then you just say "this was good but it didn't instill anything, no feelings, whatsoever in me". It's the type of book you'll carry with you after you put the book down, in your sleep, in the shower the next morning, during lunch.. To say the least, I loved it. <br /><br />Recommending it to anyone who's looking for an amazing young-adult book with lots of meaning and underlying messages.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16579578876540998833" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_782190232" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/782190232" />
    <a title="Mariam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20045084-mariam"><img alt="Mariam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470586690p2/20045084.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/782190232?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariam" href="/user/show/20045084-mariam">Mariam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18856964-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20045084-mariam?shelf=funny-reads">funny-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20045084-mariam?shelf=wow">wow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20045084-mariam?shelf=best-series">best-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer782190232" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7154618758266962440">HOLY SHITBALLS!!!<br/>OH MY GOD!<br/>I CAN'T BELIEVE THIS IS HAPPENING RIGHT NOW!<br/>I mean I can, it's called a cliffhanger but I can't believe it's happening right now, to <i>me.</i><br/>Sara Wolf, you are an evil, evil woman!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386327163ra/7339127.gif' width='400' height='202' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Let me start by saying that I'm not the biggest fan of YA. I find most of the characters annoying as hell and immature. And I rarely love YA books.<br/>NA is my thing.<br/>But I adored this book to the max! I cried, laughed, got scared shitless and picked up my jaw from the floor in the end.<br/>Because I absolu</span>
  <span id="freeText7154618758266962440" style="display:none">HOLY SHITBALLS!!!<br>OH MY GOD!<br>I CAN'T BELIEVE THIS IS HAPPENING RIGHT NOW!<br>I mean I can, it's called a cliffhanger but I can't believe it's happening right now, to <i>me.</i><br>Sara Wolf, you are an evil, evil woman!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386327163ra/7339127.gif" width="400" height="202" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Let me start by saying that I'm not the biggest fan of YA. I find most of the characters annoying as hell and immature. And I rarely love YA books.<br>NA is my thing.<br>But I adored this book to the max! I cried, laughed, got scared shitless and picked up my jaw from the floor in the end.<br>Because I absolutely love hate-to-love relationships in books, and I heard this book is funny and entertaining, I thought I'd give it a try.<br>All I can say is thank God I did. To say I loved this book would be an understatement.<br>I'll try to explain: I love this book more than I love food. Which is a big freaking deal if you ask me, because food is my first love and all.<br>I missed dinner because of this book.<br>Anyway, I loved how Jack stayed a cold asshole throughout the book. I figured he would take one look at her then chase her around like a lost puppy or something<br>But fortunately, no. He stayed a heartless asshole, and I loved him anyway.<br>Isis, Isis, Isis. I love her name, it's so unique, just like her. And what's not to love about her? She's funny as hell, sarcastic, snarky and invents weird swearing words like <i>hairy monkeyballs, dogshit on a stick, puke pancakes and many, many others.</i><br>I'll tell you what I didn't like about her; I didn't like that she was so insecure and so bent on accepting that she's ugly because some asshole who-shall-not-be-named called her that. I. Hate. Him.<br><b>
  <i>She was probably a trusting, naïve girl before him, like a daisy. And then he came, and pulled her petals off one by one, forcing her to surround herself with thorns to survive.</i>
</b><br>Isis and Jack really are like fire and ice. She's this fireball that's full of life and she's so crazy -in a good way- and she doesn't take shit from Jack, or anyone and she cares about Kayla -her friend- and her mom more than she cares about herself.<br><b>
  <i>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.”</i>
</b><br>The things they did to each other were hilarious. I was laughing my ass off at 4 in the morning. Some things were a little too far and they made me cringe and squeeze a tear or two out. But it was so engaging and kept me on my toes. Anticipating, covering one eye like watching a horror movie.<br>I loved the writing, how the author described some things. Like this one for example, Isis describing her mother's smell:<br><b>
  <i>She smells like lavender and sadness – and that smells like ripped tissue paper and sun-dried salt.</i>
</b><br>I'm still reeling from that damn cliffhanger. Normally, cliffhangers leave me rolling my eyes or not that interested in reading the next book because I know it will just drag on and on. But this one was so different, I didn't see it coming at all. Yes, I'm frustrated as hell, but I'm also dying to read the next book. Not knowing what's gonna happen is thrilling!<br>Only a month left before the sequel. I can't freaking wait. Please read this. It's different, unique and beautiful.<br>Sara Wolf, believe me when I say this: I <i>will</i> stalk you for future books. Great job, great fucking job!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/596053.gif" width="400" height="231" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7154618758266962440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
