<div id="review_2259588025" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2259588025" />
    <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews"><img alt="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1492999740p2/66199133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2259588025?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews">Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=reviews-of-the-year">reviews-of-the-year</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=hot-jerks">hot-jerks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=real-shit">real-shit</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2259588025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2162700670274013898">Well fuck me this wasn’t no silly love story, it was a <b>rip-your-goddamn-heart-out-and-stomp-on-it-for-fun</b> story. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“He has no idea who I am. He has no idea what I’ve been through.<br/>He’s an idiot. But then again, most people are.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282232.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Meet <b>Isis Blake</b>. I’m 1000% convinced she is certifiably insane and i totally support her <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Because I’m strong. Because I’m Isis Blake, and she might not be pretty, or sweet, or well-mannered, but she’s very, very strong.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282233.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was some of the realest fucking shit </span>
  <span id="freeText2162700670274013898" style="display:none">Well fuck me this wasn’t no silly love story, it was a <b>rip-your-goddamn-heart-out-and-stomp-on-it-for-fun</b> story. <br><br><b>
  <i>“He has no idea who I am. He has no idea what I’ve been through.<br>He’s an idiot. But then again, most people are.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282232.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Meet <b>Isis Blake</b>. I’m 1000% convinced she is certifiably insane and i totally support her <br><br><b>
  <i>“Because I’m strong. Because I’m Isis Blake, and she might not be pretty, or sweet, or well-mannered, but she’s very, very strong.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282233.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was some of the realest fucking shit i have ever read. jesus christ <b>the feels were off the charts</b>. There were sentences in this book that physically made my heart stop and just think. <b>I swear to god i had like 5 existencial crisis. </b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ll be the daughter they want me to be until I figure out the person I want to be.”</i>
</b><br>I saw myself on these pages. I had no idea who i wanted to be, what my own thoughts were so I just agreed with family because it was easier and I just didn’t have room for myself at the time<br><br>With her weirdass name Isis tries to fuck everyone up but meets her match with <b>Jack Hunter the local prick.</b> Honestly its like they both sociopaths or something which was awesome. It was low key juvenivlle the way they hated each other but holy shit they went at each other it was <i>bloodthirsty</i> and just amazing.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Frigid blue eyes blaze with the coldest fire I’ve ever seen, the face they belong to carved in shadow and rage.<br>I squeak and shield myself. “Leave a pretty body for my mom.”</i>
</b><br><br>Her POV was so strong and hilarious but emotional and just so well written: <br><br><b>
  <i>“The counter guy burps. “Uh, that guy just threw a chip at you.”<br>“He’s mad I won, good sir.” I sigh happily. “And he’s mad because he realized I’m going to keep on winning. It’s what I do.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282234.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Plus she totally calls high school life out on its shit:<br><b>
  <i>“There are only two things people will ask you in your senior year of high school: what colleges you’re applying to and whether or not you have a boyfriend. Everything else seems completely irrelevant. No one will ask after your mental state (deteriorating rapidly with all my homework and essays)</i>
</b><br><br>HOW FUCKING REAL IS THIS?!?! Literarly no one cares about anything except those two questions of boyfriends or college, because once they have those answer they’ll go back to focusing on themselves<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282235.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And of course enter the cliche Best Friend. Some secondary character as someone for us to compare the main character to:<br><b>
  <i>“Oh, thank God, Kayla. Your fabulous ass is intact! The stability of world peace depends on that ass”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282236.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then Jack pretending to love secondary best friend but it was fake and no one knew and oh my god my fucking heart<br><br><b>
  <i>“Jack is being patient and humorous and gentle, everything Kayla wants him to be. He’s mirroring her. <u>It’s not the real him, but she’s so in love with it she can’t see that.</u><br>It’s sad.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183073ra/25282237.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now this asshole, <b>Jack Hunter</b>. Again each character begins with high school cliches to make you dismiss them THEN THEY DO A TOTAL 180 <b>AND IT FUCKS YOU UP</b> AND WHY DID I EVER THINK HE WAS A NORMAL SANE BOY<br><br>The war between Isis and Jack was literarlly the greatest thing i have ever read and so entertaining: <br><br><b>
  <i>“JACK HUNTER SAID I’M beautiful. There is only one conclusion as to what must be done.<br>Jack Hunter’s gotta die.”</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183074ra/25282238.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I often found myself arguing with the fictional character Jack, AND I WAS WINNING DAMMIT<br><br>And the <b>romance</b> like it was such an antagonizing slow burn i wanted to fucking beat their asses till something happened but then once it did and like hell nothing goes as planned and this book refelcted that<br><br><b>
  <i>“That’d kinda suck to die over something as stupid and idiotic as love. Here Lies a Stupid Little Girl, Who Collapsed Into a Casual Ball of Panic and Pitiful Sobs at the Idea of Love. P.S. Cupid Won This Round, Sucka”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183074ra/25282239.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Welcome to my <u>book boyfriend club</u>, Jack Hunter you prick<br><br><b>
  <i>“Then don’t! Don’t trust me. Don’t trust anyone! That’s the way you like it, right? That’s the way you’ve been moving through life for the past three years, right? It’s obviously working for you, so keep doing it. Have fucking fun trusting nobody for the rest of your life!” he roars.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522183074ra/25282240.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall I greatly underestimated this novel, but Lord I have seen the light and this book is amazing. I can’t wait to continue the series. Cuz you know some dark shit is about to go down</span>
  <a data-text-id="2162700670274013898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2690301891" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2690301891" />
    <a title="Brittany " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29560188-brittany"><img alt="Brittany " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605650642p2/29560188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2690301891?book_show_action=true">Jan 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brittany " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brittany " href="/user/show/29560188-brittany">Brittany </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=5-star-reads">5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=year-2019">year-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29560188-brittany?shelf=book-crack">book-crack</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2690301891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17210792067491355741"><b> 5 Stars!! </b><br/>🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><br/><b> <i>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.” </i></b><br/><br/>Isis hasn't fell in love in over 3 years. Because of what happened last time, she has no plan to ever do it again. Since then, she has lost weight, changed her hair, and moved to Ohio to help her mom with a bad relationship.<br/><br/>Enter Jack Hunter. AKA the Ice Prince. Everyone at school wants him but h</span>
  <span id="freeText17210792067491355741" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars!! </b><br>🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><br><b> <i>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.” </i></b><br><br>Isis hasn't fell in love in over 3 years. Because of what happened last time, she has no plan to ever do it again. Since then, she has lost weight, changed her hair, and moved to Ohio to help her mom with a bad relationship.<br><br>Enter Jack Hunter. AKA the Ice Prince. Everyone at school wants him but he doesn't give anyone the time of day. Hes been spotted downtown with older women. He never gives high school girls a second glance- that is until Isis punches him in the face. GAME ON. <br><br>I was not expecting to like this as much as I did!! This is just the book I needed to get out of a bit of a book slump. I had a huge book hangover and this pulled me right out of it. <br><br>Isis is sooo annoying but hilarious at the same time. She is clever and calculated but she also has some really deep hurts she needs to deal with. Jack has a HUGE secret too and Isis is determined to find out what it is and win this war between them. I loved their banter and the sarcasm in this book is over the top, but oh so glorious. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Come! Come sit by me. It’s a nice bench. Nice and lovely on the butt.” “You’re drunk.” “Yeah, and you’re ugly, but do I complain about it? No! Because I don’t complain about things that I can’t change. That’s called intelligence.”</i>
</b> <br><br>The plot was well thought out and the dialogue is probably one of the best I have ever read. Its so unique and different. There is no insta-love.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1548611742ra/26977444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isis and Jacks relationship builds over many obstacles. And Jack is an ass throughout the whole book, and pretty much stays that way.. but it works. It also deals with a lot of dark and heavy issues and really draws you in. I could not put this book down. <br><br>That ending though-<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503964125ra/23709694.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The cliffhanger was freaking devastating yet at the same time, EPIC. I just love Sara Wolf and her ability to plug me into her worlds. I immediately had to pick up book 2 and I'm almost done with it as well! RTC for that soon! Totally recommend !!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17210792067491355741" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1122037356" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1122037356" />
    <a title="•Anna•" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21107091-anna"><img alt="•Anna•" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429128944p2/21107091.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1122037356?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="•Anna•" class="user" itemprop="url" name="•Anna•" href="/user/show/21107091-anna">•Anna•</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1122037356" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2865768582941278068">Actual Rating: A HUNDRED MILLION STARS!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426965641ra/14140144.gif' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>THIS. BOOK.<br/>I swear, I'll try being coherent, I'll even try explaining you the magnificence of this book! <br/>GEMMA YOU WERE SO RIGHT, BTW.<br/><br/><b>SARA WOLF I TOTALLY WORSHIP YOU.</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>I reach out for his hand, my own trembling. His fingers look so long and slender, and gentle. They feel smooth, and warm. I take hold of a few of them, like they're a lifeline. A raft in the sea. A rope in a deep hole.<br/>“You smell good,” I say. “And you’re fun to pick on. And I like your mom. </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2865768582941278068" style="display:none">Actual Rating: A HUNDRED MILLION STARS!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426965641ra/14140144.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THIS. BOOK.<br>I swear, I'll try being coherent, I'll even try explaining you the magnificence of this book! <br>GEMMA YOU WERE SO RIGHT, BTW.<br><br><b>SARA WOLF I TOTALLY WORSHIP YOU.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I reach out for his hand, my own trembling. His fingers look so long and slender, and gentle. They feel smooth, and warm. I take hold of a few of them, like they're a lifeline. A raft in the sea. A rope in a deep hole.<br>“You smell good,” I say. “And you’re fun to pick on. And I like your mom. You’re smart. Kind of dumb, but also kind of smart. I had fun. With the war. And the kiss. And the date. And you called me beautiful and it was nice. So even if we never battle again, even if you hate me forever for saying I like you, thank you."</i>
</blockquote><br>I stumbled upon this book (seriously, I didn't even know I had it) because I was looking for something really good, funny, heart-stopping and all that stuff. MISSION ACCOMPLISHED! Oh my, I completely lost track of the time and it was absolutely awesome. This book is a freaking amazing page-turner and you people should know what I'm talking about, so make some changes in your schedule and go read it. RIGHT NOW. <br>I feel so damn euphoric, it's like Isis infected me with her craziness. <br><br><b>ISIS.</b><br>This girl, guys. This girl cracked me up. The way she talked to people and everything she did made me laugh so hard. She's that amazing. My new fav character. I just loved everything about her. Honestly. <br>She's so tough on the outside, but so vulnerable on the inside.<br>While reading her story I thought of what they say, you know, about hilarious people. Maybe they had a sad past and they experienced something big, so they try their best to forget about that, smile all the time, make other people smile, and go on. That is what Isis is. She says a lot of crazy, funny things, always blabbering about someone's poop, throwing dog poop at Jack's car. BUT. She's broken, and keeps trying to fix people around her.<br><br>At East Summit High Isis is the "New Girl", nobody knows her but she's a tornado, and soon draws everybody's attention. She lost her trust in people when <i>Nameless</i> hurt her but that didn't stop her. We get to know her past and the whole thing behind Nameless' story towards the end of the book. And then you just stop laughing, your heart stops beating for a sec, cry a little, and you don't know whether you're misinterpreting the truth or not.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I'm not empty. I'm still a person. I cried over a bad thing that happened in my life, but I probably shouldn't have.<br><br>I've kept it inside this long.<br>I can do it for a lot longer.<br>Because I'm strong. Because I'm Isis Blake.</b>
</blockquote><br><b>JACK.</b><br>He's the Ice Prince of ESH. He doesn't talk to people. They're just annoying, meaningless, stupid living things to him. When he hurts Kayla's feeling, Isis gets so mad she starts a very competitive (and oh so fun!) war with him. He's arrogant and impossible, and I swear, YOU'RE GONNA LOVE THEIR CONVERSATIONS.<br><br><br>This book doesn't stand out from the others for its originality. I mean, a girl with a trauma who changes to start over and meets this hot, rude guy? But the thing is the author deals with all these clichés with an amazing humor that makes you laugh your lungs out... these crazy people you'll inevitably fall in love with... <b>I MEAN, I READ ALL THE ACKNOWLEDGMENTS! THAT MUST MEAN SOMETHING!</b><br><br>And Jack... he's asdfghjkl and I love the way he talks to Isis, the way they think to hate each other. He's such an asshole at the beginning, but whatever.<br>And ---- SPOILER ---- he's an escort.<br>Oh, and that cliffhanger is unthinkable. <br><b>#BYE</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I cannot, for the life of me, remember what we were just conversing about! Alas. I will forever remember this time we spent together affectionately and oh god I remember now you pervert!”<br>“You were the one who shouted ‘sex’!” He hisses.<br>“You were the one who was born, so really I think that’s the root of the problem."</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="2865768582941278068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_766236962" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/766236962" />
    <a title="preppea" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5812482-preppea"><img alt="preppea" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369597935p2/5812482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/766236962?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="preppea" class="user" itemprop="url" name="preppea" href="/user/show/5812482-preppea">preppea</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=zz-reviewed">zz-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=zz-i-love-this">zz-i-love-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5812482-preppea?shelf=humor">humor</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer766236962" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14248879134700358327">A Cliffhanger? A CLIFFHANGER? How did I miss this? How did I get to 99% and still not have a clue until I saw the word “acknowledgements”? I swear if it hadn’t been the middle of the night and my husband hadn’t been sleeping beside me I would have been doing this…<br/><br/><a href='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EyLpb8SKXlU/UrErSLB5FgI/AAAAAAAAAuk/oETG4Kw9YY8/s1600/ron-swanson-computer-throw-out-parks-and-rec.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img height='184' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387344076ra/7581323.gif' width='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>The story was just too great and the cliffhanger too drastic for me to just… sit here and WAIT for book#2! Waah! <br/><br/><a href='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1IHREkGrtX8/UrEsSBBHPYI/AAAAAAAAAuo/1Or86UaBMm8/s1600/baby-cry.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387344076ra/7581324.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Sara Wolf solidified herself in my mind with LOVELY VICIOUS as an author to watch. I’d read the first two books in </span>
  <span id="freeText14248879134700358327" style="display:none">A Cliffhanger? A CLIFFHANGER? How did I miss this? How did I get to 99% and still not have a clue until I saw the word “acknowledgements”? I swear if it hadn’t been the middle of the night and my husband hadn’t been sleeping beside me I would have been doing this…<br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EyLpb8SKXlU/UrErSLB5FgI/AAAAAAAAAuk/oETG4Kw9YY8/s1600/ron-swanson-computer-throw-out-parks-and-rec.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="184" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387344076ra/7581323.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The story was just too great and the cliffhanger too drastic for me to just… sit here and WAIT for book#2! Waah! <br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1IHREkGrtX8/UrEsSBBHPYI/AAAAAAAAAuo/1Or86UaBMm8/s1600/baby-cry.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387344076ra/7581324.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sara Wolf solidified herself in my mind with LOVELY VICIOUS as an author to watch. I’d read the first two books in her ARRANGED series and thoroughly enjoyed the characters—but LOVELY VICIOUS was a step above. Sara Wolf combines hilarious humor and witty dialogue for a story that had me constantly alternating between rolling on the floor laughing and sitting on the edge of my seat waiting to see what would happen next.<br> <br><blockquote>I’m desperate for friends, not socially suicidal. There’s a fine, pathetic line between the two and I’m toeing it like a ballet dancer at her first recital.</blockquote><br><blockquote>It’s light green and rusted, with a broken headlight and soda cans littering the floor, but it does its job of letting everyone know I’m poor and that’s really all I ask from a car.</blockquote><br><blockquote>“No. Unlike you, I have a life to attend to. I can’t afford to waste my time arguing the fine points of what makes you an idiot.”</blockquote><br>Isis is a walking contradiction. Her self-esteem is 10 notches below sea level yet she speaks with confidence, snark, and self-deprecating witticism that keeps even the most popular kids in school engaged. She has a heart of gold and will do anything, including punching a guy and making his life hell, to protect someone she cares about. She’s convinced she will never, ever experience love or intimate relationships personally, but even in her lowest moments she fights to stay positive and strong. She is observant, smart, and can run circles around most of the kids her age. <br><br>Jack is an enigma. No one knows him. He is the ice prince of the school and refuses to lower himself to even acknowledge others at his school, yet everyone wants to know him, be with him. Something about Isis forces him to fight back and engage when he’s accustomed to blocking it all out. They are equals in intelligence and observation. He is a mystery in so many ways. A knight in shining armor for a girl named Sophia, the reader can tell there might be a heart buried under all that ice but he also has a dark past that hints at danger and violence. My favorite thing about Jack was that he wasn’t just the typical jerk and as soon as you got to know him, you saw his cold personality hid a well-kept secret and a heart of gold. He is committed to his role as asshole/ice prince and doesn’t deviate – it will truly take someone special to cross the Grand Canyon that is the defensive moat around his heart.<br><br>Most importantly, Isis can’t take another heartbreak, so no matter how intriguing Jack might be, I was so terrified to see her get hurt again. Not all secrets are revealed in the first book in the Vicious series and certainly not all wounds are mended and I am in giddy anticipation of SAVAGE DELIGHT! <br><br>LOVELY VICIOUS is a great book for anyone who likes a strong heroine who won’t let anyone silence her. I can’t imagine anyone not falling in love with Isis’ incredible personality and witty, snarky humor.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14248879134700358327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1386358738" />
    <a title="Vasiliki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32039736-vasiliki"><img alt="Vasiliki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454678710p2/32039736.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1386358738?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vasiliki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vasiliki" href="/user/show/32039736-vasiliki">Vasiliki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781633752306" href="/book/show/25671748-love-me-never">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32039736-vasiliki?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32039736-vasiliki?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1386358738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10806029715782292908">5 stars!!!!!!<br/><br/><i> ARC kindly provided by <b> Entangled Publishing, LLC </b> via Netgalley in exchange of an honest review. </i><br/><br/>This is the story of Isis, the new girl! Isis who came from Florida to Ohio and she wants to make a new start leaving everything behind her. Somehow she stars a war with Jack aka Ice Prince.<br/><br/>This story is so much more than what I just described. This is a story full of emotions and love! Love on so many different levels! Most of all, this story is about pure and innocent love! I laughed</span>
  <span id="freeText10806029715782292908" style="display:none">5 stars!!!!!!<br /><br /><i> ARC kindly provided by <b> Entangled Publishing, LLC </b> via Netgalley in exchange of an honest review. </i><br /><br />This is the story of Isis, the new girl! Isis who came from Florida to Ohio and she wants to make a new start leaving everything behind her. Somehow she stars a war with Jack aka Ice Prince.<br /><br />This story is so much more than what I just described. This is a story full of emotions and love! Love on so many different levels! Most of all, this story is about pure and innocent love! I laughed out-loud, I cried, I was breathless and I mended a broken heart during this journey. The plot moves fast and is full of secrets, surprises and twists. Some of the secrets come out but most of them don't! The story is said from Isis' POV with a couple of chapters said from Jack's POV. The writing of Ms. Wolf is so alive and vivid, just amazing!<br /><br />Isis is not an usual teenager. She would like to be but she is not and she has accepted. She is fire actually. She speaks her mind without thinking and she doesn't care what the others think. Of course all these are just her armor against pain and hurt. Inside Isis has a huge and innocent heart! I just love her!<br /><br />Jack is also unusual as teenager. He is cold and distant and nothing attracts his interest. He has a purpose and he is focus only to that. I love him too because I know that all this actions are guided also by love.<br /><br />Isis and Jack are actually two sides of the same coin in my mind. I love their war and their interactions! They are so intense and so true!<br /><br />The last chapters of the book were just mind-blowing! I really didn't see coming any of the events that took place! I was speechless! The end of this book was a huge cliff-hanger that I cannot stop thinking about! Wonderful story!!<br /><br />I definitely recommend this book to everyone who likes to read about pure and innocent love!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10806029715782292908" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Gaby (lookingatbooks)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38181422-gaby-lookingatbooks"><img alt="Gaby (lookingatbooks)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529528646p2/38181422.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1139251132?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gaby (lookingatbooks)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gaby (lookingatbooks)" href="/user/show/38181422-gaby-lookingatbooks">Gaby (lookingatbooks)</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26077450-love-me-never">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38181422-gaby-lookingatbooks?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1139251132" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7990361575708253146"><b>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.” </b><br/><br/><i>Reread #3</i><br/><br/>Well, it's about time someone wrote a book that's completely unique and piqued my interested. There is nothing like Vicious Lovely. It's a fresh book about a girl who protects herself with an armor of… wait for it: insults and jokes. <br/><br/>Isis Blake is a character anyone can fall for. She's spunky, quirky, ri</span>
  <span id="freeText7990361575708253146" style="display:none"><b>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.” </b><br /><br /><i>Reread #3</i><br /><br />Well, it's about time someone wrote a book that's completely unique and piqued my interested. There is nothing like Vicious Lovely. It's a fresh book about a girl who protects herself with an armor of… wait for it: insults and jokes. <br /><br />Isis Blake is a character anyone can fall for. She's spunky, quirky, risqué. And the epitome of how girls could act if they forgot the cliches and what society expects, acting like their true self. . So naturally Isis has become my favorite character in the history of all characters! <br /><br />The story is based off of pain and how the main character drives herself to forget her past hurt. I found Isis to be a relatable character in some instances and to shock me other times. This book is loaded with random thoughts and run-on sentences, something that sets it apart from other books. I can't categorize this story, for it has every thing from love to downright wars where bird crap is being smeared on the others windshield. It's one of the craziest things I've read so far. And mind you, I'm a romance reader ;)<br /><br />Should I bring up Jack Hunter? That conversation might be a little… spontaneous. So to say. The Ice King may be my weakness. He's cold but then he's warm. It's like that game you played as a kid, where you're tagging your friends to find out if they're hot or cold, safe or unsafe. It's annoying but adventurous in all its glory. <br /><br />One thing is for certain, Sara Wolf is a true talent.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7990361575708253146" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2704819658649048410">Reread: 2020<br/><br/>I am beyond glad Goodreads recommended this book to me. This book was so much fun to read and oh man that ending!!!<br/><br/>Isis is a girl moved to a new town which means a new high school. At a party one night she sees Jack work his horrible self on someone and she felt the need to stand up for them. Well Isis and Jack have just met each other’s match. Her way of staking her claim of a boy- hating-self-proclaimed-bad-girl; was to literally punch Jack in the face. BOOM. And there it begins.<br/><br/>At</span>
  <span id="freeText2704819658649048410" style="display:none">Reread: 2020<br /><br />I am beyond glad Goodreads recommended this book to me. This book was so much fun to read and oh man that ending!!!<br /><br />Isis is a girl moved to a new town which means a new high school. At a party one night she sees Jack work his horrible self on someone and she felt the need to stand up for them. Well Isis and Jack have just met each other’s match. Her way of staking her claim of a boy- hating-self-proclaimed-bad-girl; was to literally punch Jack in the face. BOOM. And there it begins.<br /><br />At first I wasn’t sure if I was going to like Isis but she totally grew on me. Sure she has some issues but man I loved her sassy-sarcastic self! She used to be fat so she has stretch marks, her thighs jiggle and she calls herself ugly. But she has accepted who she is and has accepted the fact that she thinks she’s ugly. However I can understand how she would think she was ugly and never again would want to be touched by a man. After being bullied and tricked she has decided to completely change herself and who she use to be so she will never ever have to experience that again. Sadly that includes never falling in love…again.<br /><br />Jack has issues of his own, I liked him. Sure, was he an absolute jerk? yes. did he need to be? no. Is he perfect? no. Did I have issues with him? sure! But overall, his jerk-y-ness was his defense wall. He is tired of being treated and fawned, and even pawed at all the time from women. So to keep them away he treats them badly by using their weaknesses and insecurities against them. Horrible right? But I found him and his interaction with Isis intriguing so I kept going.<br /><br />One of my biggest problems I have with his story? His chosen “secret” life he has outside of high school. Do I understand? sure, doesn’t mean I have to agree with the author’s choice of lifestyle. Just throwing that out there.<br /><br />But what made this book so worth the read was the action going on between both Jack and Isis and how they went about each other. I absolutely loved the funny side of Isis that wasn’t there at first but slowly built over time with the story till by the time I finished the book I was chuckling out loud and smiling! I love books that can make me do that! Plus that crazy cliffhanger and the fact that I am absolutely DYING to get my hands on book two!!! AAAHHH! I can’t wait!<br /><br />So Overall I enjoyed it, I did have some issues with it, but overall I really enjoyed it.<br /><br />Sexual Content: moderate/heavy<br />Language: heavy<br />Violence: moderate<br />Drugs/Alcohol: moderate/heavy</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12000118232893491656"><i>Lovely Vicious</i> viciously took my heart and stomped all over it. I loved this book so god damn much. I'm sad it's over but I am more than happy to dive into that second book.<br/><br/>Isis Blake is probably the most insane character you will ever meet. However, I feel in love with her instantaneously. She is also a god damn bad ass. I could probably just write this review all about how I love her. Okay, I'll go on. Isis is such a god damn bad ass that she will fuck up anyone she meets. Well, until she meet</span>
  <span id="freeText12000118232893491656" style="display:none"><i>Lovely Vicious</i> viciously took my heart and stomped all over it. I loved this book so god damn much. I'm sad it's over but I am more than happy to dive into that second book.<br /><br />Isis Blake is probably the most insane character you will ever meet. However, I feel in love with her instantaneously. She is also a god damn bad ass. I could probably just write this review all about how I love her. Okay, I'll go on. Isis is such a god damn bad ass that she will fuck up anyone she meets. Well, until she meets Jack Hunter. He is also crazy in the mind but I ended up loving the little shit too. When they went at each other, I'm pretty sure I had my creepy smile plaster on my face. Like, go on please. I need more from you two!<br /><br />Besides all of that awesomeness, Isis's POV was gold. I laughed so hard and when I wasn't laughing I was probably having mini heart attacks. My favorite thing from her was when she talked about high school. I couldn't decided if I should laugh or give her props because it's so fucking true.<br /><br />This book will call you out on your bullshit and the bullshit of the other characters - I loved it!<br /><br />Besides that, there's Kayla. The best friend. Jack basically pretends to like her and no one fucking knows about it! MY HEART MAN. I was like.. don't love him woman. WALK AWAY WOMAN. Of course, no one in the book heard my sweet words but I still loved the shit out of him and his assholeness.<br /><br />Overall, the war between Isis and Jack was the best thing ever written. I need more. I want more. Where is the second book when I need it?!?! The romance was such a slow burn and a little bit enjoyable - but this girl right here is impatient as fuck. This romance was like a pedestrian walking in the cross walk in front of your car.. taking their sweet ass time to get to the other side. Meanwhile I'm freaking out and frustrated as fuck because I'm not a patient person. At one point I will yell out my window, "KNEES TO CHEST BITCH, KNEES TO CHEST!" just to motivate them to walk faster. If that doesn't work, the horn is a nice touch too.<br /><br />Loved the book. Loved Isis so freaking much. I NEED MORE! </span>

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390339030ra/8194055.gif" alt="shut up photo tumblr_inline_mjl9cqJupx1rbumi6_zps9c12df38.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She has sworn off love because of Nameless who totally ruined her. She sees Jack Hunter, aka Ice Prince, one night at a party. Jack is a conceited asshole and all the girls fall over him.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385269892ra/7114014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isis gets pissed when she sees him be rude to her new friend, Kayla. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/7627903_zpsc4506a4b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390339030ra/8194056.gif" alt=" photo 7627903_zpsc4506a4b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>You see, Kayla is the first friend Isis has ever really had and Jack is totally rude to her so she declares war on him.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390339030ra/8194057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their war is pretty messed up....a rumor, public kiss, fat pics posted around school, drugs in a locker, small dick rumors, etc. etc etc...I kept waiting for something to go down with the animal she sleeps with at night, Mr. Muffins or whatever....<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385781618ra/7226595.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Through her hate for Jack she winds up liking him. (You know that is gonna happen) And she winds up kissing him at a party but of course she's drunk....<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mlfefaQZSZ1s78ry7o1_250_zps09e2673a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/583961.gif" alt="JENNA photo tumblr_mlfefaQZSZ1s78ry7o1_250_zps09e2673a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will say I was a little annoyed with the whole thing about her getting him to take Kayla on a date and then Isis throwing up and him then taking her to eat Sushi? Wasn't she just puking her guts up? And you want to feed her Sushi??<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390339030ra/8194058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then towards the end when the drama goes down, Jack just happens to be there to apologize.....<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/coincidence-i-think-not-incredibles_zps14106244.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388288481ra/7788578.gif" alt=" photo coincidence-i-think-not-incredibles_zps14106244.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I didn't know this book had a cliffhanger and honestly the cliffhanger pissed me off. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ How can she remember every single person except Jack?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/482278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will likely read book two though to find out what happens between Jack and Isis.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1688882228" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1688882228" />
    <a title="Sarah (thegirltheycalljones)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32607699-sarah-thegirltheycalljones"><img alt="Sarah (thegirltheycalljones)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1569607878p2/32607699.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1688882228?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah (thegirltheycalljones)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah (thegirltheycalljones)" href="/user/show/32607699-sarah-thegirltheycalljones">Sarah (thegirltheycalljones)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sarah (thegirltheycalljones) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/20712926-gelisvb">Gelisvb</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32607699-sarah-thegirltheycalljones?shelf=puh-leeze">puh-leeze</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32607699-sarah-thegirltheycalljones?shelf=stupid-mc">stupid-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32607699-sarah-thegirltheycalljones?shelf=douche-fest">douche-fest</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1688882228" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11776173916624975791">What the holy fuck? That was like watching <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/138202.Sloppy_Firsts__Jessica_Darling___1_' title='Sloppy Firsts (Jessica Darling, #1) by Megan McCafferty' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sloppy Firsts</a> collide with Pretty Little Liars and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28678119.Paper_Princess__The_Royals___1_' title='Paper Princess (The Royals, #1) by Erin Watt' rel='nofollow noopener'>Paper Princess</a> at hyperspeed, providing a massive splash of glittery blood. It's shiny, but it's also slimy.<br/><br/>I highly enjoyed the first half. Isis, our MC, is very funny and I mean it. I highlighted many quotes and laughed out loud many times. It reminded me a lot of Sloppy Firsts : a smart and witty heroin who's not the most beautiful girl ever but who manage to survive high school thanks to her sharp t</span>
  <span id="freeText11776173916624975791" style="display:none">What the holy fuck? That was like watching <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/138202.Sloppy_Firsts__Jessica_Darling___1_" title="Sloppy Firsts (Jessica Darling, #1) by Megan McCafferty" rel="nofollow noopener">Sloppy Firsts</a> collide with Pretty Little Liars and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28678119.Paper_Princess__The_Royals___1_" title="Paper Princess (The Royals, #1) by Erin Watt" rel="nofollow noopener">Paper Princess</a> at hyperspeed, providing a massive splash of glittery blood. It's shiny, but it's also slimy.<br /><br />I highly enjoyed the first half. Isis, our MC, is very funny and I mean it. I highlighted many quotes and laughed out loud many times. It reminded me a lot of Sloppy Firsts : a smart and witty heroin who's not the most beautiful girl ever but who manage to survive high school thanks to her sharp tongue and some self-mockery.<br />She was the real asset of this book, by far!<br />The Love Interest, Jack, is a mix between Reed Royal (Douchy) and Marcus Flutie (My Official Dream Guy). He was okay in the beginning (the Marcus Flutie part) but he turned out to be a bit boring (the Douchy part). I didn't get the swoon in the end but he filled the bill up to a certain point.<br />The secondary characters were not original one bit but in the first part it was okay : I had the feeling to watch a cartoon with clichéd-on-purpose character. It was a <a href="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/8/8c/Recess_poster_toon.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">Recess</a> with teenagers! (I <i>adore</i> Recess, so it's a big fat compliment here)<br />The banter was very good, almost everything coming out of Isis mouth is hilarious, expect when she just babbles and turns exasperating but it doesn't last, she often comes back with a strong line!<br /><br />Then, the second part happened.<br />What the fucking fuck?<br />An over-dramatic shitstorm hits the town and it was like someone grabbed the book I was reading, tossed it out of the window and put a new one in my hands instead, asking me to pretend it was the same book.<br />That's the Pretty Little Liars part I was talking about. So many implausible and/or over-the-top elements were thrown in there... Think of every drama tropes you know, and now think about every drama tropes you <i>don't know</i>. Now think about more drama. There, you have it.<br />I can't say more without being spoilery but COME. ON. You can't force drama and more mature contents in a book being light and pure fun. It's like...it's like <a href="http://richestcelebrities.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/Honey-Boo-Boo-Net-Worth.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">Honey Boo Boo</a>. It feels wrong.<br /><br />As I still have to mention one specific element that I genuinely HATE, here's a spoiler tag :<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[MOTHERFUCKING AMNESIA. LIKE REALLY?! ISIS CAN'T REMEMBER JACK AFTER BEING BEATEN UP BY HER MOM'S PSYCHO EX (yes, I told you, drama and it's only a part of it)! AMNESIA. I FUCKING HATE AMNESIA. And of course, she doesn't remember Jack only, the rest is fine. Talk about plot-convenience... AMNESIA FFS! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />So, it started as a light but very fun book and it ended up with me ranting about it. Disappointment.<br />Jessica Darling is eternal. Isis Blake isn't.<br /><br />Gelis: Can't wait to read what you think about it once you'll be finished! Maybe we can still read book 2 together if you can cope with my rant... <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11776173916624975791" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/852395186?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="If it ain&#39;t good I don&#39;t read it !" class="user" itemprop="url" name="If it ain&#39;t good I don&#39;t read it !" href="/user/show/8370340-if-it-ain-t-good-i-don-t-read-it">If it ain&#39;t good I don&#39;t read it !</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer852395186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9951375827015882304">Let me just say i just knew this book would be awesome by just reading the Authors name and the blurb. I mean seriously Sara <i>Wolf</i>. Do you know how awesome you have to be to pull off that last name. <br/><br/><i>Sara Wolf</i><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392236987ra/8523752.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>lol, Anyways cool ass last names aside I'd just like to say I loved this book. Seriously whats there to not like, it was funny as hell, fast paced and without any of that usually bullshit teen dramaz shit that makes up almost every other teen book i try to read. I mean can i get a eye roll?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383167265ra/6424196.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I</span>
  <span id="freeText9951375827015882304" style="display:none">Let me just say i just knew this book would be awesome by just reading the Authors name and the blurb. I mean seriously Sara <i>Wolf</i>. Do you know how awesome you have to be to pull off that last name. <br><br><i>Sara Wolf</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392236987ra/8523752.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>lol, Anyways cool ass last names aside I'd just like to say I loved this book. Seriously whats there to not like, it was funny as hell, fast paced and without any of that usually bullshit teen dramaz shit that makes up almost every other teen book i try to read. I mean can i get a eye roll?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383167265ra/6424196.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Isis Blake has to be one of the few teens I've read about that i didn't plan mental murder for while reading.<i>Heck</i> i loved the chick!!<br><i>“I cannot, for the life of me, remember what we were just conversing about! Alas. I will forever remember this time we spent together affectionately and oh god I remember now you pervert!”<br>“You were the one who shouted ‘sex’!” He hisses.<br>“You were the one who was born, so really I think that’s the root of the problem.”</i> <br><br>Talk about a breath of fresh air, and her feud with Jake<br><br><b>priceless</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491919682ra/22461981.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But that wasn't even it, wasn't what really sold me on this book. I liked that Isis battled her own demons, i loved that she could make you cry as much as she could make you laugh. I loved that the characters were raw and real, i loved that Sara kept us on our toes guessing what it was that happened and reveled everything yet nothing at the same time. Point being <b>I Loved this Book</b> period. <br><br><br>That being said WTF was with that ending??<br><br>I mean i feel like... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411193ra/807179.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Frankly i don't like it, The sad thing is i saw it coming, in some deep, deep sense i knew it was going to end in a cliffhanger, and when it finally did i was the picture of a mental patient yelling at my Ipad. Trying to stop the inevitable. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422880ra/841934.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>yeah</i>.....<br><br> <br>- 5 kick ass stars</span>

<div id="review_3032246219" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3032246219" />
    <a title="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen"><img alt="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1575851043p2/42276702.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3032246219?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kenzie The Dragon Queen" href="/user/show/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen">Kenzie The Dragon Queen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18657517-lovely-vicious">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=books-i-have-reviewed">books-i-have-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=body-diversity">body-diversity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42276702-kenzie-the-dragon-queen?shelf=feminism">feminism</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3032246219" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18026394716023609099"><b>
  <i>“There are only two things people will ask you in your senior year of high school: what colleges you’re applying for and whether or not you have a boyfriend. Everything else seems completely irrelevant. No one will ask after your mental state (deteriorating rapidly with all my homework and essays), what you do to have fun (stare at my bedroom ceiling and pick nail polish off my nails), or whether or not you actually want to go to college (no, I don’t, I’m tired of school, but I’ll go because </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText18026394716023609099" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“There are only two things people will ask you in your senior year of high school: what colleges you’re applying for and whether or not you have a boyfriend. Everything else seems completely irrelevant. No one will ask after your mental state (deteriorating rapidly with all my homework and essays), what you do to have fun (stare at my bedroom ceiling and pick nail polish off my nails), or whether or not you actually want to go to college (no, I don’t, I’m tired of school, but I’ll go because everyone is making me and flipping burgers at McDonald’s for seven bucks an hour sounds revolting).”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Wow! So this book was a delightful surprise! I didn’t expect it to be so good. ‘Lovely Vicious’ or ‘Love Me Never’ (the title is different depending on the format, don’t ask me why) was a wildly witty, heartrending, funny, blood pumping, and surprisingly thought provoking and poignant book.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’m fuelled by rage and at least seven cupcakes made by someone’s talented mother.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I loved Isis Blake, she was hilarious and so relatable. Her jovial sense of humour made reading the story through her eyes 400% better. I loved all her snappy comebacks, sarcastic one-liners, weird and lengthy tangents, and funny inner dialogue that sometimes turned into actual dialogue because she didn’t realize she was thinking out loud.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Wow, sorry, I was fabulously thinking aloud again, I do that a lot, look, could you get me the noodles?”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />The author was able weave sinfully witty banter, dialogue, and monologue into her story, so seamlessly, it all slid together naturally, without coming off as too flashy or too cheesy. The comedic pacing of this book was dead on, and the overall humour was a major highlight of this book.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“No. Unlike you, I have a life to attend to. I can’t afford to waste my time arguing the finer points of what makes you an idiot.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />The banter between Isis and Jack was so genuinely witty and thoroughly entertaining. The chemistry between them was evident from the very beginning, but only got stronger and better as the story went on. And don’t even get me started on the enemies to lovers slow burn! These two were at each other’s throats at the beginning of the book, and the slow burn was so slow, it made the small things that would eventually make them reach the “lovers” part, that much better! I’m not kidding when I say this is a serious slow burn. It’s so deliciously slow, you won’t believe it until you read it.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’m currently devising terribly fiendish torture scenarios in which Jack doesn’t get out alive with his penis intact.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I surprised myself when I found that I actually liked Jack as a character? I don’t really feel drawn to the dark brooding loner types, I find them kind of boring, and almost always more two dimensional then they ought to be. But Jack doesn’t entirely fit into the “dark brooding loner” category. Jack is SO salty, and so sarcastic, and his macabre sense of humour was the perfect foil against Isis’ over the top jovial snark and farce.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You’re like him” she repeats. “Jack. You’re different. People can feel it. That’s why you two are at odds, probably. You’re so similar. Like two magnets repelling each other.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />I really enjoyed the relationships built in this novel. Characters seemed to develop friendships with each other naturally, and not just because the book demanded it. Also, I absolutely loved Isis and Kayla’s friendship. Sometimes, it reminded me of Leslie and Anne’s friendship from ‘Parks and Recreation’. Mostly because Isis acted a little like Leslie with how protective and loving she was towards sweet innocent Kayla.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Oh Kayla, you gorgeous, sugary, incredibly fluffy butterfly,”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Okay, now we move onto the slightly more serious stuff. I really liked how the author handled Isis’ character in relation to her weight, or rather, her previous weight. As someone who’s suffered from anorexia for years, I didn’t feel at all trigged, and I didn’t feel like the fact that Isis was skinny, in any way insinuated that she was a lesser person when she was fat. I thought the entire topic of body image, and how we perceive beauty (in ourselves and in others), was handled really well. On one hand, Isis thinks she’s ugly (which isn’t true), and that’s just how life is for her. On the other hand, although it isn’t explicitly said, Kayla and Jack are a little tired of being reduced to nothing except “attractive” because no one can look past that and see how kind Kayla is and how smart Jack is. I thought it was poignant of the author to present a girl that clearly has body dysmorphia due to trauma, and put her in a situations with people that don’t want to be reduced to simply “pretty” and allow her to be exposed to different individuals. It had more impact then just having her slowly realize she wasn’t ugly. I really appreciated that even though Isis isn’t fat anymore, she doesn’t see her past self as worse or bad for being fat. No, the author made it clear that Isis’ was never lesser for once weighing more.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I have to do this for myself. For the girl in the picture. If there’s anything I’ve learned this year, it’s that I have to stand up for myself, or no one else will.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />The issue of trauma, PTSD, depression, abuse, and insinuation of rape and suicide, was also touched about quite delicately in this book. This part is a little harder for me to dissect. It’s one of those things you’ll just have to read for yourself to understand. Nevertheless, I thought the author handled these issues tactfully, and with an informed and compassionate perspective. The story never seemed to take advantage of any of these issues for the sake of entertainment, and I appreciate that greatly. Once again, I didn’t find myself triggered by these topics, which is somewhat an indicator that they were neither too prominent or exploitative. At least, I personally didn’t feel like they were.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Sometimes, we can’t do the things we want to do for ourselves. Sometimes we wait for someone else to do them. You can’t always wait like that. You have to seek out change on your own.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Oh, off topic, but the ending was one giant slap to the face. It felt like cheating to me, or just lazy writing. Anyway, my point is it seemed like a plot device, but only the sequel and time will tell if it was a good one or not. In my opinion, it was cheap trick, meant to create unnecessary and over the top angst, but to each their own. It also felt very dramatic and unrealistic. I guess I shouldn’t have been too surprised by that, because there is another dramatic and unrealistic element to this book, but if I told you what it was, that would be a spoiler. It’s not like that specific element or the ending it is so outrageous you won’t believe it, it’s just a little bit soap opera sixth season of a CW show where their running out of content so they throw in a random aspect that’s shocking enough to keep their viewership entertained, for better or worse. Does that make sense?<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I laugh. “Jesus, you’re a piece of work.” “And you’re not? I’ve never met a more stubborn, jaded, cynical girl in my life.” “It’s true. I’m very special.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Overall, this novel was an incredibly addicting, entertaining, funny, and heart pumping extreme enemies to lovers slow burn. Full of poignant backdrop morale, enjoyable witty banter, humorous writing, and a heart-pounding central romance, ‘Love Me Never’ / ‘Lovely Vicious’ is undoubtedly worth a read!<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“And that’s the story of how I was recruited to become a cat burglar by Satan.”</i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18026394716023609099" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wcZXoChQ0Y0dDYjE/5zk/7tb8uYdRfVP4wGk/+OzycxhOFDru0nk14TDdncgPjcu2GPje8nd7TIeZ1C6WbJqHQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Pw93Lw5tnFks6CZ1aKeXiGndwSweW8+Fs04lTSylFL+f8XBknXSpA7Um2Ma3BURZCuXQscrD1/hOKNEIlqS3bg==')})
